ADDITIONAL NOTES
A. NOTES
Precipitation utiIized during winter months to meet forage freshwater requirements.
Irrigation weIls TID 12, 15, 17, 28, 44, 54, 56, 57, 58, 60, 91, 121, 122 & 124 were non-operational or not used in 2023. AIl weIls wiIl be sampIed once the weIls
become operational and/or used during the cropping season. Heavy rains during the winter season aIlowed for a greater amount of surface water aIlocation to
grow crops.
FieIds T204, 205, 301, 302, 303/306, 304, 305, 1107, & 1108 AImonds had lower than anticipated removal rates due to lower than anticipated YN or low
tonnage. This resuIted in fieId ratios sIightIy exceeding target limits.
FieIds T201 Tomatoes, T903 AImonds, & T904 AImonds had lower than anticipated removal rates. This was due to lower than expected yieIds and/or a lower
than expected N. The N was based on anaIysis that was derived through a certified laboratory. However, the appIications to these fieIds matched the low
removal rates and was abIe to meet the fieId ratio threshoId of 1.4.
FieIds T1001, 1003-1009 Rye Grass had higher than anticipated removal rates. This was due to much higher than expected N and/or yieId. The N removed,
which is based on anaIysis derived through a certified laboratory, exceeded the anticipated vaIues for this crop. Appropriate management practices resuIted in
decent yieIds and/or higher than expected nutrient removal rates.
Nutrients appIied to permanent crops, such as trees and vines, are used for tree growth, vine deveIopment and fruit production (grapes, nuts, etc.). Comparing
nutrient appIications to nutrient content of harvested material for permanent crops is not appropriate and wiIl resuIt in high fieId ratios. A more accurate reporting
methodoIogy wiIl need to be deveIoped in order to account for nutrients retained in the permanent crops. AIl appIications wiIl continue to be monitored cIoseIy to
ensure that over appIication of nutrients does not occur.
FieIds T903-905 AImonds received no wastewater or soIid manure in 2023. AIl nutrients appIied to these fieIds were contributed through freshwater appIications
and/or commercial fertiIizer onIy.
FieIds T101-104 & 905 AImonds are newIy pIanted aImonds and therefore had no production in 2023.
FieIds 1102 & 1104 AImonds were removed after harvest 2022 and were faIlow for fieId work during the winter season 2023.
FieIds T1101-1105 were faIlow during the winter cropping season 2023. FieIds T901 & 902 were faIlow 2023.
